{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01Sn4mvMb5CDYDLvDaZ9SdsF","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"thinking","thinking":"Perfect! Now I understand the pattern. The `Client[T]` type in `gentype` implements the basic methods like:\n- `Get(ctx context.Context, name string, options metav1.GetOptions) (T, error)`\n- `Create(ctx context.Context, obj T, opts metav1.CreateOptions) (T, error)`\n- `Delete(ctx context.Context, name string, opts metav1.DeleteOptions) error`\n\nAnd `alsoLister[T, L]` implements:\n- `List(ctx context.Context, opts metav1.ListOptions) (L, error)`\n\nThe pattern is quite clear now. ],\n    82→  \"text\": \"The implementation of a typed Kubernetes custom resource (CRD) client for the Widget resource (group example.com, version v1) follows the established patterns in the kubernetes client-go codebase. The core design draws from the kubernetes/typed/core/v1 package structure, specifically from configmap.go and core_client.go which define interface-based clients for Kubernetes resources. The rest.Interface from rest/client.go provides the foundational REST communication layer used by all typed clients. The gentype/type.go package contains the generic Client[T] type helper which implements the fundamental Create, Get, Delete, and List methods using the rest.Interface and context.Context propagation patterns. For CRD implementations, the APIPath is set to '/apis' (as shown in kubernetes/typed/apps/v1/apps_client.go) rather than '/api' (used for core resources). The configuration setup follows setConfigDefaults pattern which sets the GroupVersion, APIPath, and NegotiatedSerializer using rest.CodecFactoryForGeneratedClient. Each typed client struct embeds rest.Interface, and implements methods that chain REST operations: Post() for Create, Get().Name() for Get, Get() for List, and Delete().Name() for Delete operations. All methods accept context.Context as the first parameter after the receiver to support cancellation and timeout propagation.
